          (bn2): BatchNorm2d(512, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
        )
      )
      (avgpool): AdaptiveAvgPool2d(output_size=(1, 1))
      (fc): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=1000, bias=True)
    )
  )
)
